<rating>4<//rating><review>So I saw the reviews and decided to give this place a try. I enjoy ramen alot so of course I had to see if this place measures up to my usual spot in Glendora. Walked in and was greeted and sat right away. Our server was very nice and polite. I order their volcano ramen medium spicy and the rest of my party ordered salmon sashimi tuna sashimi, dynamite roll, and Philadelphia roll. Everything was great! The volcano ramen broth was super good and it had a good kick to it. I was very pleased. The sushis were also very good and fresh. I'm giving this place 4 out of 5 only because we were the only group there and it took them a bit to get the sushi out. Also I ordered spicy tuna roll and they completely forgot about it. I'd totally come back for ramen.<//review>< pictures>
